1200px) 100vw, 1200px" width="600" height="150"/>\n</picture>\n</noscript></a></div></div><p>The Swanage Railway has announced that it will run a series of new Coronavirus-safe &#8216;Steam and Lights&#8217; festive trains during the run up to Christmas.</p>\n<p>Operating on ten days, with two evening trains, the new service will replace the Swanage Railway&#8217;s Santa Specials, which cannot operate due to the coronavirus pandemic.</p>\n<p>Instead of Father Christmas handing out presents to children, the new service will see trains covered in coloured lights as they steam through the Isle of Purbeck in the dark.</p><div class="raila-content" id="raila-1761735856"><script data-rocketlazyloadscript=\'//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js\' async ></script>\n<ins class="adsbygoogle" style="display:block;" data-ad-client="ca-pub-1855742918545992" \ndata-ad-slot="3703639860" \ndata-ad-format="auto"></ins>\n<script data-rocketlazyloadscript=\'data:text/javascript;base64,IAooYWRzYnlnb29nbGUgPSB3aW5kb3cuYWRzYnlnb29nbGUgfHwgW10pLnB1c2goe30pOyAK\' ></script>\n</div>\n<p>There will also be special displays at stations, as well as other locations along the 5-mile heritage railway. Trains will run from Swanage to Corfe Castle and Norden for a one hour return trip.</p>\n<p>Before passengers board the train at Swanage, there will be a dramatic switch on of the lights on the platform.</p>\n<p>Swanage station will only be open to Steam and Lights passengers, whilst Herston Halt, Harman&#8217;s Cross, Corfe Castle and Norden will be closed to the public.</p><div {"header_icon":"","first_title":"Related","second_title":"Posts","url":"","header_type":"heading_6","header_background":"","header_secondary_background":"","header_text_color":"","header_line_color":"","header_accent_color":"","header_filter_category":"","header_filter_author":"","header_filter_tag":"","header_filter_text":"All","post_type":"post","content_type":"all","number_post":"2","post_offset":0,"unique_content":"unique1","include_post":"","exclude_post":"69216","include_category":"","exclude_category":"","include_author":"","include_tag":"990,1516","exclude_tag":"","post_tag":"","event_location":"","event_organizer":"","event_type":"","event_type_2":"","event_type_3":"","event_type_4":"","product_cat":"","product_tag":"","sort_by":"latest","date_format":"default","date_format_custom":"Y\\/m\\/d","force_normal_image_load":"","pagination_mode":"nextprev","pagination_nextprev_showtext":"","pagination_number_post":"2","pagination_scroll_limit":0,"boxed":"","boxed_shadow":"","el_id":"","el_class":"","scheme":"","column_width":"auto","title_color":"","accent_color":"","alt_color":"","excerpt_color":"","css":"","paged":1,"column_class":"jeg_col_2o3","class":"jnews_block_20"};</script>\n            </div>\n            </div>\n                    </div>\n<p>The Swanage Railway volunteer Commercial Director Steve Williams said: \xe2\x80\x9cThis new \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 train service in the run-up to Christmas is a festive first for the Swanage Railway and we are very excited because it will be very special and out of this world \xe2\x80\x93 colourful, evocative and dramatic. We are looking forward to it tremendously.</p>\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cThe need to keep our passengers and staff safe against the threat of Covid-19 \xe2\x80\x93 by following social distancing and the wearing of face coverings \xe2\x80\x93 means that we cannot run our traditional, and very popular, Santa Special trains where Father Christmas gives presents to children on the train and has his photograph taken.</p>\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cWith the help of an experienced and reputable company specialising in synchronised lighting and music, we have been working very hard to design a special festive train service that will make wonderful and magical memories for children and adults in the run-up to Christmas,\xe2\x80\x9d added Steve.</p>\n<p>Steam and Lights trains will operate on the first two weekends of December and then daily from Friday, 18 to Wednesday, 23 December 2020, with departures from Swanage station at 5.15 pm and 7.15 pm.</p>\n<p>Steve explained: \xe2\x80\x9cAt the time of booking, passengers can purchase a special festive picnic box filled with tasty treats and drinks to make their \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 journey extra special.</p>\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cA memorable experience suitable for all ages, stations and key points along the line will be specially lit as the \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 train passes through in the dark. On board the train, there will be festive music synchronised to the lighting displays passing the carriage windows as well as an informative on-train commentary.</p>\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cWith allocated socially distanced seating, the \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 trains must be booked in advance and can only be joined at Swanage station where the brightly lit festive trains start and end their journeys.</p>\n<p>\xe2\x80\x9cTo comply with Government health regulations, no bookings can be taken for groups comprising more than six people and face coverings should be worn on the platform at Swanage station as well as on the \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 train,\xe2\x80\x9d added Steve.</p>\n<p><div class="rll-youtube-player" data-src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/-vLSaHoWa1s" data-id="-vLSaHoWa1s" data-query=""></div><noscript><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/-vLSaHoWa1s" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen"></iframe></noscript></p>\n<p>Swanage station shop will be open when Steam and Lights are running, subject to volunteer availability.</p>\n<p>Tickets for the \xe2\x80\x98Steam and Lights\xe2\x80\x99 trains are \xc2\xa320 each for passengers aged 15 and above, \xc2\xa315 for children aged three to 15 and free for children aged under three if they sit on an adult lap.</p>\n<p>A maximum of six people can be booked on one booking.</p>\n<p>To book your tickets, please <a href="http://swanagerailway.co.uk/events/detail/steam-lights">click here</a>\xc2\xa0to visit the Swanage Railway website.</p>\n<h3>Where Next?</h3>\n<p><a class="btn btn-default" style="background-color: #990000; color: white;" trains with special Steam and Lights event","name":"Swanage Railway replaces Santa steam trains with special Steam and Lights event","articleBody":"The Swanage Railway has announced that it will run a series of new Coronavirus-safe \'Steam and Lights\' festive trains during the run up to Christmas.\\r\\n\\r\\nOperating on ten days, with two evening trains, the new service will replace the Swanage Railway\'s Santa Specials, which cannot operate due to the coronavirus pandemic.\\r\\n\\r\\nInstead of Father Christmas handing out presents to children, the new service will see trains covered in coloured lights as they steam through the Isle of Purbeck in the dark.\\r\\n\\r\\nThere will also be special displays at stations, as well as other locations along the 5-mile heritage railway. Trains will run from Swanage to Corfe Castle and Norden for a one hour return trip.\\r\\n\\r\\nBefore passengers board the train at Swanage, there will be a dramatic switch on of the lights on the platform.\\r\\n\\r\\nSwanage station will only be open to Steam and Lights passengers, whilst Herston Halt, Harman\'s Cross, Corfe Castle and Norden will be closed to the public.\\r\\n\\r\\nThe Swanage Railway volunteer Commercial Director Steve Williams said: \\u201cThis new \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 train service in the run-up to Christmas is a festive first for the Swanage Railway and we are very excited because it will be very special and out of this world \\u2013 colourful, evocative and dramatic. We are looking forward to it tremendously.\\r\\n\\r\\n\\u201cThe need to keep our passengers and staff safe against the threat of Covid-19 \\u2013 by following social distancing and the wearing of face coverings \\u2013 means that we cannot run our traditional, and very popular, Santa Special trains where Father Christmas gives presents to children on the train and has his photograph taken.\\r\\n\\r\\n\\u201cWith the help of an experienced and reputable company specialising in synchronised lighting and music, we have been working very hard to design a special festive train service that will make wonderful and magical memories for children and adults in the run-up to Christmas,\\u201d added Steve.\\r\\n\\r\\nSteam and Lights trains will operate on the first two weekends of December and then daily from Friday, 18 to Wednesday, 23 December 2020, with departures from Swanage station at 5.15 pm and 7.15 pm.\\r\\n\\r\\nSteve explained: \\u201cAt the time of booking, passengers can purchase a special festive picnic box filled with tasty treats and drinks to make their \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 journey extra special.\\r\\n\\r\\n\\u201cA memorable experience suitable for all ages, stations and key points along the line will be specially lit as the \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 train passes through in the dark. On board the train, there will be festive music synchronised to the lighting displays passing the carriage windows as well as an informative on-train commentary.\\r\\n\\r\\n\\u201cWith allocated socially distanced seating, the \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 trains must be booked in advance and can only be joined at Swanage station where the brightly lit festive trains start and end their journeys.\\r\\n\\r\\n\\u201cTo comply with Government health regulations, no bookings can be taken for groups comprising more than six people and face coverings should be worn on the platform at Swanage station as well as on the \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 train,\\u201d added Steve.\\r\\n\\r\\n<iframe src=\\"https:\\/\\/www.youtube.com\\/embed\\/-vLSaHoWa1s\\" width=\\"560\\" availability.\\r\\n\\r\\nTickets for the \\u2018Steam and Lights\\u2019 trains are \\u00a320 each for passengers aged 15 and above, \\u00a315 for children aged three to 15 and free for children aged under three if they sit on an adult lap.\\r\\n\\r\\nA maximum of six people can be booked on one booking.\\r\\n\\r\\nTo book your tickets, please <a
